Lazzaretto is basically the Italian term used to describe the place where people where quarantined during the period of the Black Plague. If you visit Venice, (I live in there, it is a mess) there's an island disposed as such. It is really beautiful, but that place has a really grim aura when you visit it. Still there's no guardian keeping the place in order, it is said there are restless ghosts around that place.

Ghostemane, I know im a day late but I wanted to give you all my support and to let you know that I needed to hear this and see this to get through a really hard time in my life,  and its crazy you have shown up when I really needed it and had nobody, not even my own family. Honestly, your work has impacted me and given me an outlet when I had nowhere else to go. I suffer from PTSD, anxiety, crippling depression and ive never ever been able to freely talk about this but from the bottom of my heart you are my hero. You saved me from a dark place, you helped me realize I am never alone, and that its okay to express how you feel. For so long I was critised into thinking it was bad to feel negative feelings and never was able to emotio ally connect to others. I relate to feeling numb and dissassociating and I feel like you send amazing messages that only those know just know. You have come so far and don't ever stop. Your music helps keep me going, and you really have brought a new meaning into my life I have been missing and thats to truly be yourself. I love the realness of it. So thank you, and keep making BANGERS MY DUDE. Also congrats on being engaged to Poppy, she is amazing and everything you and her deserve.

I mean, you can only get it so low... and bass guitars can be distorted as well totally bypassing the need for a super heavy gauge guitar string anyway.

Claim your 'here before the russians' ticket
I'll preface by saying i think with the direction these songs have shown him going, this album could be my favourite.  additionally, eric's standard is so high, and so many of his songs are my favorite that to say one is better than another doesnt mean any of them suck by any means.  that said, there are at least 4-5 songs off each n/o/i/s/e and hexada respectively that i like much better than this and probably AI. Neither of these releases are likely top 10 ghoste songs for me. I prefer AI to this song, although the quick 'ugh-ugh-ugh" part that shows up twice in this song is up there with my favourite bits of audio he's created.    I hope he doesnt stray too far into metal, even tho id say i might prefer metal to hip hop overall, tho barely, i think eric's strength lies in blending the two in such a unique way.  the NIN influenced songs are awesome, and eric is clearly a massive Trent fan, as am i.  I love the songs where he combines both the hip hop and metal tho, almost equally, where one isn't totally dominating the other.  Both songs are amazing, way better than nearly anything else coming out right now.   Ghostemane is arguably my favourite music project of the last few years (Nihil being one of my 5 favourite songs of the 2010s, i am so happy that song exists. seriously, thanks eric), along with POPPY funny enough, and was the case before they even started dating.  I am always chomping at the bit for anything new from eric, tho. He's probably the most consistent artist going right now, out of whom I listen to.  there are songs by others that have come out that are up there with some of his stuff, but the whole project isn't as good.  eric never misses, and even tho i have favourites i can truly listen to his last few albums from front to back and listen to his singles that didn't make the album as much as any song on the album, if not more.    So psyched to have someone exactly my age, from my generation, who has been through so much of the same psychological things i have to make music that speaks so directly to me, what i feel, how i feel it, and how i feel about feeling it.
